Based on the error logs and the user's requirement, here are the diagnostics and suggested fixes:

### Error Analysis

1. **`log.blockMesh` Error**:
   ```
   ERROR: 
   Trying to specify a boundary face 4(3 2 6 7) on the face on cell 0 which is either an internal face or already belongs to some other patch.
   ```
   This error indicates that the face `4(3 2 6 7)` assigned to the `hotWall` patch is incorrectly specified. It appears that this face is either an internal face or is already part of another patch, which violates OpenFOAM's mesh topology rules.

2. **`log.buoyantFoam` Error**:
   ```
   ERROR: 
   Cannot find file "points" in directory "polyMesh" in times "0" down to constant
   ```
   This error occurs because the mesh was not successfully generated due to the previous error in `blockMesh`. Without a valid mesh, OpenFOAM cannot proceed with the simulation.

### Root Cause

The root cause of the first error is likely in the `blockMeshDict` file where the `hotWall` patch includes a face that conflicts with another patch or is an internal face. Specifically, the face `4(3 2 6 7)` might be incorrectly defined or overlap with another patch definition.

### Suggested Fixes

#### Fix 1: Correct the `blockMeshDict`

In the `blockMeshDict`, ensure that each face is uniquely assigned to one patch and does not overlap with others. The current definition of the `hotWall` patch may be incorrect. Let’s verify and correct the `blockMeshDict`:

1. **Check Face Definitions**: Ensure that the faces listed for each patch are unique and do not overlap.
2. **Correct `hotWall` Patch Definition**: The face `(3 2 6 7)` should not conflict with other patches. In the provided `blockMeshDict`, the `hotWall` patch is defined as:
   ```foam
   hotWall
   {
       type wall;
       faces
       (
           (3 2 6 7)
       );
   }
   ```
   This face corresponds to the top face of the block, which is shared between `front` and `back` patches. If the `front` and `back` patches also include this face, then it's a conflict.

   **Fix**: Adjust the `front` and `back` patches to exclude the face `(3 2 6 7)` so that only `hotWall` owns it.

   Example correction:
   ```foam
   front
   {
       type patch;
       faces
       (
           (0 1 5 4)
       );
   }

   back
   {
       type patch;
       faces
       (
           (2 3 7 6)
       );
   }

   hotWall
   {
       type wall;
       faces
       (
           (3 2 6 7)
       );
   }
   ```

#### Fix 2: Regenerate the Mesh

After correcting the `blockMeshDict`, regenerate the mesh using:
```bash
blockMesh
```
Ensure that the command completes without errors.

#### Fix 3: Verify Mesh Generation

Once the mesh is successfully generated, check if the `points` file exists in the `constant/polyMesh` directory:
```bash
ls constant/polyMesh/points
```
If the file exists, proceed with the simulation.

#### Fix 4: Run Simulation

With a valid mesh, run the simulation using:
```bash
buoyantFoam
```
